            <section class="large-9 medium-12 small-12">
                <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
                    <header class="article-header gutter-right-off">
                                            <h1 class="entry-title single-title" itemprop="headline">Two more poultry workers test positive for avian influenza</h1>
                    </header>
                    <div class="hide-small-down">
                      <div class="pm-save-article-wrap"></div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="article-content">
                        <div class="article-meta hide-large">
                            <div class="author-meta">
                                <span class="author-name"><a href="https://www.fwi.co.uk/author/philip-case">Philip Case</a></span>

                                <span>&gt;More in</span>
                                <span class="border-bottom"></span>
                                <ul><li><a href="https://www.fwi.co.uk/livestock/poultry">Poultry</a></li></ul>                            </div>

                                                  <div class="featured-image gutter-bottom gutter-top">
                            <img width="900" height="506" src="https://stmaaprodfwsite.blob.core.windows.net/assets/sites/1/2023/07/Broiler-chickens-c-tim-scrivener-web.jpg" class="attachment-large size-large wp-post-image" alt="© Tim Scrivener" itemprop="image" decoding="async" fetchpriority="high"><span>© Tim Scrivener</span>                          </div>
                                                  <div id="article-1704355-body" class="article-body">
                            <p>Two more poultry workers in England have tested positive for avian influenza, the UK Health Security Agency (UKHSA) has confirmed.</p>
<p>The two cases of bird flu have been detected at different premises in England through UKHSA’s surveillance programme of asymptomatic workers who have come into contact with birds.</p>
<p>See also: <a href="https://www.fwi.co.uk/livestock/poultry/avian-influenza-prevention-zone-lifted-but-risk-remains-2">Avian influenza prevention zone lifted, but risk remains</a></p>
<p>This means four workers have tested positive for avian flu since the programme was launched in March.</p>
<p>In May, there were two positive cases in England and those workers have since tested negative.</p>
<p>UKHSA said there were still no signs of human-to-human transmission and the level of risk to the public remains very low.</p>
<p>Dr Meera Chand, director of clinical and emerging infections at UKHSA, said: “Current evidence suggests that the avian influenza viruses we’re seeing circulating in birds around the world do not spread easily to people.</p>
<p>“However, we know already that the virus can spread to people following close contact with infected birds,” she said.</p>
<p>“And this is why, through surveillance programmes like this one, we are monitoring people who have been exposed to learn more about these risks.”</p>
<p>As of 10 July 2023, 144 people from eight infected premises have been tested through enhanced surveillance of poultry workers.</p>

                    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
                        function inject_mideditorial(type='mpu-1',size='',every=3,skip='',lazyload=0, limit=1000)
                        {
                            let content = document.querySelectorAll('#article-1704355-body > p');
                            let count = 0;
                            let ad_count = 0;
                            every = every-1;
                            if(every<1)
                            {
                              every=0;
                            }
                            if(skip)
                            {
                                skip=skip.split(',');
                            }
                            
                            if(!Array.isArray(skip))
                            {
                                skip=[];
                            }
                            
                            if(content instanceof NodeList)
                            {
                                let total = content.length;
                                let advertObserver = false;
                                let function__loadAdvert = function(target){
                                    let type=target.getAttribute('data-type');
                                    let size=target.getAttribute('data-size');
                                    let i=target.getAttribute('data-no');
                                    let advert=pm_adverts.getHTML(type,type,size);
                                    target.innerHTML=advert.body;
                                    content[i].append(target);
                                    pm_adverts.runCallback(advert.id, function(me, adUnit, event){
                                        if(('size' in adUnit) && Array.isArray(adUnit.size))
                                        {
                                            me.css('width',adUnit.size[0]);
                                        }
                                    });
                                    pm_adverts.position(advert.id);
                                    console.log("PM Adverts(jQuery/inject_mideditorial):: Loaded "+type+"("+size+")["+i+"].");
                                    
                                };
                                if(lazyload)
                                {
                                    if(typeof window.IntersectionObserver !== 'undefined')
                                    {
                                        console.log("PM Adverts(jQuery/inject_mideditorial):: Can LazyLoad...");
                                        advertObserver = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries,observer){
                                            entries.forEach(function(entry){
                                                const currenty = entry.boundingClientRect.y;
                                                const currectRatio = entry.intersectRatio;
                                                
                                                if(entry.isIntersecting)
                                                {
                                                    let advert = entry.target;
                                                    console.log("PM Adverts(jQuery/inject_mideditorial):: LazyLoading...",advert);
                                                    function__loadAdvert(advert);
                                                    advertObserver.unobserve(advert);
                                                }
                                                
                                            });
                                        });
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        console.error("PM Adverts(jQuery/inject_mideditorial):: Cannot LazyLoad!");
                                    }
                                }
                                
                                console.log('inject_mideditorial',skip);
                                
                                let function__shouldSkip = function(i){
                                    if(skip.includes(""+i))
                                    {
                                      console.log("PM Adverts(jQuery/inject_mideditorial):: Skipping "+type+"("+size+")["+i+"]");
                                      return true;
                                    }
                                    if(ad_count>=limit)
                                    {
                                      console.log("PM Adverts(jQuery/inject_mideditorial):: Limit reached "+ad_count+"/"+limit+"");
                                      return true;
                                    }
                                    return false; 
                                }
                                
                                
                                
                                for(let i = 0; i < content.length; i++) 
                                {
                                    total--;
                                    if(count==every && total>1)
                                    {
                                        if(!function__shouldSkip(i))
                                        {
                                            let advert_html=document.createElement('div');
                                            advert_html.style="display:flex;justify-content:center;"
                                            advert_html.setAttribute('data-type',type);
                                            advert_html.setAttribute('data-size',size);
                                            advert_html.setAttribute('data-no',i);
                                            if(advertObserver instanceof IntersectionObserver)
                                            {
                                                content[i].append(advert_html);
                                                advertObserver.observe(advert_html);
                                                console.log("PM Adverts(jQuery/inject_mideditorial):: Lazyload "+type+"("+size+")["+i+"]");
                                            }
                                            else
                                            {
                                                function__loadAdvert(advert_html);
                                            }
                                            ad_count++;
                                        }
                                        count=0;
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        count++;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        
                                                
                        if(screen.width <= 4000)
                        {
                          inject_mideditorial('MPU-In-Article','',4,'4',1,20);
                        }
    
                    });

                        var url=jQuery(this).attr("href");
                        url = fwi_theme.addKeyValueToURL(url ,"userguid", pm_sso.get("guid"));
                        url = fwi_theme.addKeyValueToURL(url ,"returnurl", window.location.href );
                        return url;
                    }).addClass("pm-sso-guid");
                }
            }
        </script>
        
    

</body></html>
